\DoxyCodeLine{00077\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Detect\ a\ number\ of\ compiler\ features\ -\/\ mostly\ C++11/14\ conformance\ -\/\ by\ compiler}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00078\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ following\ features\ are\ defined:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00079\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00080\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_CPP11\_NULLPTR\ :\ is\ nullptr\ supported?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00081\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_CPP11\_NOEXCEPT\ :\ is\ noexcept\ supported?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00082\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_CPP11\_GENERATED\_METHODS\ :\ The\ delete\ and\ default\ keywords\ for\ compiler\ generated\ methods}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00083\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_CPP11\_IS\_ENUM\ :\ std::is\_enum\ is\ supported?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00084\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_CPP11\_TUPLE\ :\ std::tuple\ is\ supported}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00085\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_CPP11\_LONG\_LONG\ :\ is\ long\ long\ supported?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00086\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_CPP11\_OVERRIDE\ :\ is\ override\ supported?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00087\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_CPP11\_UNIQUE\_PTR\ :\ is\ unique\_ptr\ supported\ (otherwise\ use\ auto\_ptr)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00088\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00089\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_CPP11\_OR\_GREATER\ :\ Is\ C++11\ supported?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00090\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00091\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_VARIADIC\_MACROS\ :\ are\ variadic\ macros\ supported?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00092\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00093\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ****************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Note\ to\ maintainers:\ if\ new\ toggles\ are\ added\ please\ document\ them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ in\ configuration.md,\ too}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ ****************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ In\ general\ each\ macro\ has\ a\ \_NO\_<feature\ name>\ form}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (e.g.\ CATCH\_CONFIG\_CPP11\_NO\_NULLPTR)\ which\ disables\ the\ feature.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Many\ features,\ at\ point\ of\ detection,\ define\ an\ \_INTERNAL\_\ macro,\ so\ they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ can\ be\ combined,\ en-\/mass,\ with\ the\ \_NO\_\ forms\ later.}}
